3) Espectrito I DQ Máscarita Sagrada [MEX MINI]
## Match was to include Octagoncito. All three had made the finales of a 10 man elimination match on 12/18/92. Two days before the show, Octagoncito was announced as too hurt to compete (though he was still listed on spot shows.) The winner of this match would instead give Octagoncito his first defense. Seconds were Angel Blanco Jr. (Espectrito) and Alushe (Mascarita Sagrada). Blanco attacked Alushe repeatedly, Tinieblas Sr. ran in to stop that, and that was the DQ.

## About 20:00, clean match. Vampiro pinned Canek with a lariat in the 1st. Canek dropkicked, powerslammed, and sentoned Vampiro for the second fall, then Vampiro took the third for the win. Crowd hated Vampiro for winning, thought Canek was much better and booed the title change. SuperLuchas pointed to this as a breaking point for UWA, where the crowd continue to decline until the promotion closed.

AAA TV (FRI) 04/30/1993 Plaza de Toros Ciudad de México, Ciudad de México, Distrito Federal [Lucha Libre Weekly v2-12, Lucha Libre Weekly v2-13, http://youtu.be/LTc6rFwlgYk	 Roy Lucier AAA Lucha Libre, https://i.imgur.com/vuhQuG8.png SL 112]
** TripleMania
1) Martha Villalobos, Pantera Sureña, Wendy b Larrosa, Lola González, Vicky Carranza
## 17:50. Villalobos beat Gonzalez. Rosa was a last minute sub for Reyna Gallegos, who broke her leg on 03/23.
2) Salsero, Súper Caló, Winners b Baby Sharon, May Flowers, Rudy Reyna
## 11:20, Winners pinned May. Salsero's debut.
3) Misterioso, Rey Misterio Jr., Volador I b Rocco Valente, Tony Arce, Vulcano
## 13:59, Volador pinned Vulcano. Said to be the best match on the show.
4) El Hijo Del Santo, Octagón, Villano III b Fuerza Guerrera, Heavy Metal, Rambo
## 19:37, Santo submitted Metal with la de a caballo. Metal wore a t-shirt with "FUCK YOU" written in English in large letters, and the match did not air for many years as a result. It must've made it to Japan because it did turn on YouTube ventually.
5) Lizmark Sr.  (c) TLDRAW La Parka [MEX LH]
## **** 1/2*. La Parka cheated to win in 20 minutes, but the commissioner restarted the match because Tirantes fast counted. That was actually supposed to be the finish. The second match had a 15 time limit, with the idea Lizmark would have to win to keep the title. It went to a draw, but the commission gave Lizmark the title anyway. Parka was supposed to win the title.
6) Love Machine, Máscara Sagrada, Máscarita Sagrada DQ Blue Panther, Jerrito Estrada, Jerry Estrada
## 19:16, straight falls. Panther gave Machine piledriver.
7) Perro Aguayo Sr. b Máscara Año 2000 [mask]
## 21:54. Aguayo fouled Universo (Mascara's second) in one, Mascara did the same to Misterioso (Perro's second) in the second, Perro got away with a foul on Mascara in the three. Universo attacked the ref, getting himself suspended for a short time. Mascara tried to leave, but was forced to stay and unmasked by Antonio Pena, and revealed himself as Jesus Reyes Gonzalez, 35 years old.
8) Cien Caras COR Konnan [retirement]
## Jake Roberts, sitting in the crowd, challenged Konnan in the third fall. Cien got annoyed and brawled with Roberts. Jake DDTed him. Konnan shoved Jake, Cien and Konnan fought, and Jake attacked Konnan's second (Mascarita Sagrada). Konnan chased Jake around, and Mascara 2000 rolled Cien in before the bell for the win. Near riot, with fans waiting outside the arena to attack Jake until 3AM.

## Chris Jericho's book has this as a loss. SuperLuchas has this as a no contest/stopped match. Mr. Niebla was scheduled on tecnico side, Villanos put him out with a pre-match attack and Pantera (sitting in the crowd in street clothes) replaced him. Match turned into a crowd brawl and then an actual brawl with the members of the crowd; Villano V ended up bloody before the match was halted. Fans waited to fight Villano after show, police was called.
